Does giving a society to women where they cannot live on their own free will and cannot come anywhere without fear, does it not come under the purview of insensitivity? Or is killing the girl in the stomach a sign of being sensitive? sawaal man main aae ja rahe hai
 i am trying to reduce the speed of questions by strolling here and there
 kuch sawaal ab bhi meri taraf dekh rahe hai
 We are asking that if Salman Khan is insensitive, then we do not have the same insensitive Salman Khan inside us too? If Salman Khan has thoughtlessly said something that is like a wound to rape victims, how many of us have thoughtfully tried to bring some positive changes for rape victims? How much will Salman Khan's apology change? Will the people behind Salman with Boria's bed expect forgiveness from 'salman Khan' present in himself and will the 'salman Khan' within us ever apologize? tivi band kar diya he

 sab hans rahe hai

 Asking why Salman Khan has not apologized so far for his statement of 'feeling like a rape victim after training'
 kuch sawaal man main uthne lage hai
 If Salman's thinking was wrong, there was no respect for women or no pain for the rape victim, then how many of us have this respect for women or is it a pain for a rape victim? If we are all sensitive to rape victims, then why do most rape victims still go through the struggle to live a normal social life? Why even today, a large number of rape incidents are not reported for fear of finding out the society? So, is Salman Khan the same inside all of us, whom we are not ready to accept as less insensitive than his apology? man main sawaal or tezi se uth rahe hai ab
 Why are women a commodity from TV to newspaper, why are women being sold for every item sold? How many of the big editors from TV to newspaper who are raising the issue of insensitivity of Salman Khan are sensitive to the women employees of their office? kya maa-bahan kii gaali, samvedanheen hone kii catagori main nahin aata? har kaamyaab mahila kii kamyaabi ke peeche purush bos ke saath sone kii managasaint kahani duusare sahakarmiyon ko sunaanaa samvedanheen hona nahin hota? kya ek aisa samaaj mahilaon ko dena jahaan ve apni marzi se ji na saken or bina khuf kahin bhi aa ja na saken, kya yah samvedanheenata ke daayre main nahin aata? yaa bacchee ko pet me maar dena samvedansheel hone kii nishaani he?  How is the name, Masala Chai! The events that happen to new age boys happen in the backdrop of their social and personal circumstances and lack of amenities and which they like to listen to or listen to each other in another phase of life
 ' Masala Chai is the written form of the same
 skool, college, ejineering, placement, back paper, ishk, afaire, liv in, brake ap, kuch aakhri kis, train main mili anjaan ladki, english spoken class, saatvin ke bachche kaa 'balig' sawaal, apane 'eks' ke saath 'encounter', namardi kaa vigyaapan, lav marriage kii feel dene vaali arenjd marriage; or aisa hi bahut kuch

 behad aasaan bhashaa main likhi gai 176 panne kii is kitaab ko aasaani se do se teen din main padhaa ja saktaa he
